<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Who We Are: Founded in 2005, Geovision Group has consistently paved the way in developing cutting-edge solutions that streamline the sales, distribution, and marketing processes of industry giants. At our core, we are committed to optimizing resource allocation, increasing customer satisfaction, and significantly reducing operational costs by up to 25% for our customers. We are already serving industry leaders for many years and delivering the greatest value for their businesses.

Our Mission: Empower businesses with end-to-end logistics solutions that streamline sales, marketing, and logistics cycles to boost field sales performance. We ensure maximum operational efficiency with comprehensive services ranging from route optimization and fleet management to marketing strategies.

Global Reach: With our headquarters in Turkey and global offices, we serve industry leaders in achieving unparalleled operational efficiency especially for FMCG, Retail and Logistic.

Our Solutions:
- Dispatcher: Optimized last-mile delivery and fleet monitoring.
- Planner: Cost-effective sales and field team management.
- Geomarketing: Targeted market analysis and marketing strategies.
- MDM: Ensures customer data quality for accurate targeting.
- Order: Centralized order management for efficient operations.
- Scheduler: Improves team productivity and communication.

Why us?
Choosing Geovision Group means partnering with a leader in providing a synergy of services under one roof, converting sales-related data into viable business models for the FMCG industry, Logistic industry and beyond. 

Together, let's achieve greatness.

Keywords: Logistics optimization, Fleet Management, Data-Driven Strategies, SaaS, Global Operations, Cost Reduction, Geomarketing, Dispatching, Field Sales management, Offline to Online Marketing strategies, Last-mile delivery, Point of Sale (POS) analytics.

Sizleri, coğrafi verilerin stratejik avantajlara dönüştüğü özel webinarımıza davet ediyoruz! 

📅 Tarih: 14.05.2025 
🕒 Saat: 15:00 
🌐 Yer: Online (Katılım linki kayıt sonrası gönderilecektir)

* Firma Verilerinin Coğrafi Olarak Toplanması 
* Dış Verilerin Entegrasyonu 
* Distribütör Bölgelerinin Belirlenmesi 
* Pazarlama ve Satış Bölgelerinin Oluşturulması 
* Rakip Analizi ve Pazar Boşluklarının Tespiti 
* Geomarketing’te Yapay Zeka Kullanımı

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Enerjide Açık İnovasyon Demo Günü’ndeydik! ⚡

<a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/enerjisa?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Enerjisa</a>’nın ev sahipliğinde ve <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/pitgrowth?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>PitGrowth</a> iş birliğiyle gerçekleşen “Enerjide Açık İnovasyon Demo Günü” kapsamında gelecek vizyonumuzu ve çözümlerimizi paylaşma fırsatı bulduk.

Etkinlik boyunca sektör liderleri ve 20 yenilikçi girişimle bir araya gelerek sürdürülebilir uygulamalar ve olası iş birlikleri üzerine fikir alışverişinde bulunduk.

Yarının enerji çözümlerini şekillendirmenin güçlü bir kurumsal–girişim iş birliği gerektirdiğine inanıyoruz.

Davetleri ve bu değerli organizasyon için Enerjisa’ya ve Pitgrowth’a teşekkür ediyoruz.

Yeni iş birlikleri için heyecanlıyız! 🚀

✅ 𝐎𝐩𝐭𝐢𝐦𝐢𝐳𝐞 capacity &amp; 𝐝𝐢𝐬𝐭𝐫𝐢𝐛𝐮𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧 𝐩𝐥𝐚𝐧𝐧𝐢𝐧𝐠
✅ 𝐒𝐭𝐫𝐞𝐚𝐦𝐥𝐢𝐧𝐞 route scheduling &amp; 𝐝𝐢𝐬𝐩𝐚𝐭𝐜𝐡 𝐦𝐚𝐧𝐚𝐠𝐞𝐦𝐞𝐧𝐭

✅ 𝐌𝐨𝐧𝐢𝐭𝐨𝐫 performance in real-time with 𝐬𝐦𝐚𝐫𝐭 𝐚𝐧𝐚𝐥𝐲𝐭𝐢𝐜𝐬

On-Time Deliveries. Accurate Routing. Efficient Load Management

*DHL boosts customer service with geomarketing.

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Optimize Your Career Planning for Better Delivery &amp; Worker Experience
Efficient routes = Happy workers. 

When routes are optimized, you reduce delivery time and stress for your drivers. This improves job satisfaction and retention rates!

Key Benefits:
- Reduced delivery time by optimizing routes, saving fuel and costs
- Balanced workloads for drivers, leading to higher satisfaction and lower burnout
- Real-time data &amp; communication, improving efficiency and support for drivers

Case Study: VideoJoc saw a 7% improvement in operations and 10% fuel savings after implementing route optimization software!

With Geovision Dispatch Route Optimization, we help streamline logistics, save time, and boost profits. Get started now!
